<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerel.html>kerel</a> (609)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerel.html>kerel</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">carel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">caerl</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kerl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:karl.html>karl</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*karal</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*keril</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*karilaz</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kerl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_Low_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch Low Saxon">Dutch Low Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-nl">keerl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tsjirl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">churl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:karl.html>karl</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerke.html>kerke</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">kirica</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*kirikā</i>, an early borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κυριακόν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kuriakón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***kern.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kern.html>kern</a> (5023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kerne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kerno</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kernô</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kernan-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">core, kernel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵerh₂-n-on-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵr̥h₂nóm</i>, related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kurną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">corn, grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kern.html>kern</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kernen.html>kernen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kern.html>kerntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>nucleus, core</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nucleus (of an atom)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in compounds</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nuclear</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> astronomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> core (of the Earth, or any other celestial body)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> kernel (of a function)
<ul><li><b>1976</b>, "<a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eindexamen.html>eindexamen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiskunde.html>wiskunde</a> II 1976", in <i>Euclides. <a href = vnd.unilang:maandblad.html>Maandblad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> didactiek <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiskunde.html>wiskunde</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:orgaan.html>Orgaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Nederlandse <a href = vnd.unilang:vereniging.html>Vereniging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Wiskundeleraren</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 52, issue 7, Wolters-Noordhoff, 274.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bewijzen.html>bewijzen</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestaat.html>bestaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <i>k</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarvoor.html>waarvoor</a> beeldruimte <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kern.html>kern</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> A<small><sub>k</sub></small> <a href = vnd.unilang:samenvallen.html>samenvallen</a>.
<dl><dd>To be demonstrated: a <i>k</i> exists for which the image space and <b>kernel</b> of A<small><sub>k</sub></small> coincide.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2005</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:centrum.html>Centrum</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiskunde.html>Wiskunde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:informatica.html>Informatica</a>, <i>Vakantiecursus 2005. <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schijf.html>schijf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijf.html>vijf</a></i>, 55.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kijkt.html>kijkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontvangen.html>ontvangen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woord.html>woord</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kern.html>kern</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> matrix <a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>zit</a>.
<dl><dd>Therefore he <a href = vnd.unilang:checks.html>checks</a> whether the received word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> contained in the matrix's <b>kernel</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>settlement, built-up area</li></ol>

***kers.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kers.html>kers</a> (17186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kerse</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ceresia</i>, from the neuter plural of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ceresium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cerasium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κεράσιον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kerásion</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cherry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κερασός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kerasós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bird cherry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately possibly of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anatolian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Anatolian languages">Anatolian</a></span> origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Owoce_wisni.jpg/250px-Owoce_wisni.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Owoce_wisni.jpg/375px-Owoce_wisni.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Owoce_wisni.jpg/500px-Owoce_wisni.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1100" data-file-height="825" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:rode.html>Rode</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kersen.html>kersen</a></i><br />Red cherries</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kers.html>kers</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kersen.html>kersen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kersje.html>kersje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A cherry tree, one of certain trees of the genus <i>Prunus</i>, especially the subgenus <i>Cerasus</i>.</li>
<li>A cherry, a stone fruit of a cherry tree.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kerse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*kresso</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*krasjon-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gras-</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">ग्रसति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grasati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cress</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kresse</i>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Gartenkresse.jpg/220px-Gartenkresse.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="183" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Gartenkresse.jpg/330px-Gartenkresse.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Gartenkresse.jpg/440px-Gartenkresse.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1203" data-file-height="1000" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>Kresse</div></div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kers.html>kers</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>cress (watercress, garden cress), used of certain plants of the family <i>Brassicaceae</i>, esp. for plants of the genus <i>Rorippa</i> and <i>Lepidium <a href = vnd.unilang:sativum.html>sativum</a></i>.</li>
<li>nasturtium, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Tropaeolum_majus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Tropaeolum majus"><i>Tropaeolum majus</i></a></span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerstbal.html>kerstbal</a> (69322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerst.html>kerst</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstbal.html>kerstbal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstbal.html>kerstballen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstbal.html>kerstballetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A bauble (spherical decoration) used as Christmas decoration, especially in Christmas trees.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerst.html>kerst</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i>.

***kerstdag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerstdag.html>kerstdag</a> (16672)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerst.html>kerst</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstdag.html>kerstdag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstdagen.html>kerstdagen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Christmas Day</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In plural, the term refers to the days of Christmas, in particular Christmas Day and Boxing Day. These are referred to as <i><a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerstdag.html>kerstdag</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tweede.html>tweede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerstdag.html>kerstdag</a></i> in Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstdag.html>kerstdag</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li>25 december, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarop.html>waarop</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:christenen.html>christenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:christus.html>Christus</a>' <a href = vnd.unilang:geboorte.html>geboorte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:feestelijk.html>feestelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:herdenken.html>herdenken</a>.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>Wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstdag.html>kerstdag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belangrijke.html>belangrijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:herdenkingsdag.html>herdenkingsdag</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li>één <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> kerstfeestdagen.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tweede.html>tweede</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstdag.html>kerstdag</a></b>!</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerstman.html>kerstman</a> (2190)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerst.html>kerst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Christmas</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstman.html>kerstman</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstman.html>kerstmannen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstman.html>kerstmannetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Father Christmas, Santa Claus</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The figure of Santa Claus <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not native to Dutch culture, and the term generally refers to the Anglo-Saxon depiction. To Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> the name <i>Saint Nicholas</i> refers to Sinterklaas, who distributes presents to children on the eve or day of December 6, not at Christmas.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kerstman.html>kerstman</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:verouderde.html>verouderde</a> spelling of <a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerstman.html>Kerstman</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> vóór 2006</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerstman.html>Kerstman</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:speelt.html>speelt</a></li></ol>

***ketch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ketch.html>ketch</a> (82229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">catche</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">cacchen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to catch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. For the modern form with <span class="IPA">/ɛ/</span>, compare the pronunciation <span class="IPA">/kɛtʃ/</span> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">catch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ketch.html>ketch</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ketches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fore-and-aft rigged sailing vessel with two masts, main and mizzen, the mizzen being stepped forward of the rudder post.
<ul><li><b>1720</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Daniel_Defoe" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Daniel Defoe"><a href = vnd.unilang:daniel.html>Daniel</a> Defoe</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Captain_Singleton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Captain Singleton"><a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>Captain</a> Singleton</a></i>, London: J. Brotherton et <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>., p. 313,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/lifeadventurespy00defo">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> to finish her new Habit or Appearance, and make her Change compleat, he ordered her Sails to be alter’d; and as she sailed before with a Half-Sprit, like a Yacht, she sailed now with square Sail and Mizen Mast, like a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ketch.html>Ketch</a></b>; so that, in a Word, she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> Cheat <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">catch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ketch.html>ketch</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">ketches</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ketching</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ketched</b>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Eye dialect spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">catch</i></span></span>.

<dl><dd>I guess, he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> trying to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ketch.html>ketch</a></b> mebut it <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> du. I'm tu old a bird to be <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ketch.html>ketch</a>'d</b> with chaff.</dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd>You'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ketch.html>ketch</a></b> your death. The fire's out long ago.</dd></dl></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***keten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:keten.html>keten</a> (11148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ketenen.html>ketene</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ketina</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">catēna</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">ketina</i> (German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kette</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:keten.html>keten</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ketenen.html>ketenen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ketens.html>ketens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:keten.html>ketentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>chain, fetter, shackle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chain (of events or businesses)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:keet.html>keet</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fool around noisily and hyperactively</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:keu.html>keu</a> (17018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">queue</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tail, queue, cue</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
